User: What is mathematics?
Assistant: Mathematics is the study of numbers and shapes. It uses logic.

User: What is addition?
Assistant: Addition combines numbers. For example, 2 plus 3 equals 5.

User: What is subtraction?
Assistant: Subtraction takes away numbers. For example, 5 minus 2 equals 3.

User: What is multiplication?
Assistant: Multiplication is repeated addition. For example, 3 times 4 is 12.

User: What is division?
Assistant: Division splits numbers equally. For example, 12 divided by 3 is 4.

User: What is a fraction?
Assistant: A fraction shows a part of a whole. For example, one half is 1/2.

User: What is a decimal?
Assistant: A decimal uses a point. For example, 0.5 is a decimal.

User: What is a percentage?
Assistant: A percentage is out of one hundred. For example, 50 percent is half.

User: What is geometry?
Assistant: Geometry studies shapes and space. It includes points, lines, and angles.

User: What is a triangle?
Assistant: A triangle has three sides. Its angles sum to 180 degrees.

User: What is a square?
Assistant: A square has four equal sides. It has four right angles.

User: What is a circle?
Assistant: A circle is a round shape. It has no corners.

User: What is pi?
Assistant: Pi is roughly 3.14. It relates circumference to diameter.

User: What is an equation?
Assistant: An equation is a mathematical statement. It has an equals sign.

User: Solve 2 plus 2.
Assistant: 2 plus 2 equals 4. That is simple.

User: Solve 5 times 6.
Assistant: 5 times 6 is 30. Multiplication is useful.

User: What is the square root of 9?
Assistant: The square root of 9 is 3. Because 3 squared is 9.

User: What is 10 divided by 2?
Assistant: 10 divided by 2 is 5. That is a clean division.

User: What is a prime number?
Assistant: A prime number has only two factors. For example, 7 is prime.

User: Is 9 prime?
Assistant: No, 9 is composite. It factors into 3 times 3.

User: What is the Fibonacci sequence?
Assistant: It starts 0, 1, 1, 2, 3, 5, 8. Each term sums the previous two.

User: What is algebra?
Assistant: Algebra uses letters for numbers. It solves for unknowns.

User: What is calculus?
Assistant: Calculus studies change. It has derivatives and integrals.

User: What is physics?
Assistant: Physics studies matter and energy. It covers motion and forces.

User: What is gravity?
Assistant: Gravity pulls objects together. It keeps us on Earth.

User: What is light?
Assistant: Light is electromagnetic radiation. It travels in waves.

User: What is sound?
Assistant: Sound is a vibration. It travels through air.

User: What is energy?
Assistant: Energy is the ability to do work. It comes in many forms.

User: What is electricity?
Assistant: Electricity is the flow of electrons. It powers devices.

User: What is a magnet?
Assistant: A magnet attracts iron. It has a north and south pole.

User: What is an atom?
Assistant: An atom is the basic unit of matter. It has protons and electrons.

Assistant: A molecule is two or more bonded atoms. For example, water is H2O.
